// File added: plugins/logger/index.html
function writefile_11() {
	@$fp = fopen('plugins/logger/index.html', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('plugins/logger/index.html') && (sha1_file('plugins/logger/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/logger/index.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/logger/index.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/logger/index.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/logger/index.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_11();
if (!is_file('plugins/logger/index.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/logger/index.html');
} else if (sha1_file('plugins/logger/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/logger/index.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/logger/index.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/logger/index.html');
}

	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php') !== 'a5c2c3ba199b1611aaeeb0cd5a197e480a0e444d') {

		writefile_13();

if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') != 'ee25a236fd335d9bd78e6c004adcd6c0b785b5d7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'ee25a236fd335d9bd78e6c004adcd6c0b785b5d7') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'b42ba5355cf728cff192126315c013e9dc25aa18') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'ee25a236fd335d9bd78e6c004adcd6c0b785b5d7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/files') != '7806e38fad4fc4bb79ea16317fb9cc59f79f99b1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/files');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/files', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/files');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/files') !== '7806e38fad4fc4bb79ea16317fb9cc59f79f99b1') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/files') !== '9555d26d739b39875e7e23aefde516b4bcc796bb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/files');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/files');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/files')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/files', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/files') !== '7806e38fad4fc4bb79ea16317fb9cc59f79f99b1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/files');
		}
	}
}
